<t>CREATE TABLE employees ( id UUID PRIMARY KEY, first_name STRING, last_name STRING, department STRING )

CREATE TABLE teams ( team_id UUID PRIMARY KEY, team_name STRING, team_lead UUID REFERENCES employees.id )

CREATE TABLE projects ( project_id UUID PRIMARY KEY, project_name STRING, team_id UUID REFERENCES teams.team_id )

CREATE TABLE tasks ( task_id UUID PRIMARY KEY, task_name STRING, assignee UUID REFERENCES employees.id, status STRING )</t><s>INSERT INTO employees (id, first_name, last_name, department) VALUES ('123e4567-e89b-12d3-a456-426614174000', 'John', 'Doe', 'Marketing')</s>
<t>CREATE TABLE employees ( id UUID PRIMARY KEY, first_name STRING, last_name STRING, department STRING )

CREATE TABLE teams ( team_id UUID PRIMARY KEY, team_name STRING, team_lead UUID REFERENCES employees.id )
